The Ubuntu Code of Conduct

Launchpad users can sign the Ubuntu Code of Conduct using the code of conduct page or Code of Conduct Signing Assistant. The list of Ubunteros can be found below.

The Ubuntero List

The individual and/or entities names listed below have signed the Ubuntu Code of Conduct.

The word after the full name is the Launchpad account username of the individual and/or entity. Append https://launchpad.net/~ or https://launchpad.net/people/ before the username to get the user page with more information including email, joined groups, karma, languages, time zone and more.

For tracking / identifying persons (if the Signed Ubuntu Code of Conduct value in each user page says Yes) the posted format is: entity name – Launchpad usernames.

Last update: April 6th, 2015
Total Ubunteros: 17,293
